***deliverance.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:deliverance.html>deliverance</a> (31983)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:deliverance.html>deliverance</a></i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">délivrance</i>), <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">delivrer</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-ance</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:deliverance.html>deliverance</a></strong> (<i>countable <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">deliverances</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:act.html>Act</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> delivering <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> conveying <a href = vnd.unilang:something.html>something</a>.</li>
